                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 97, -73, 2;
                                } else {
                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }

                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }

                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 75, -73, 2;
                                }
                            } else InInventory PowerFlight || PowerSpeed {
                                InInventory PowerInvulnerable
                                {
                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }

                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }

                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 75, -73, 2;
                                } else {
                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }

                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }

                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 53, -73, 2;
                                }
                            } else {
                                InInventory PowerInvulnerable
                                {
                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }

                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }

                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 53, -73, 2;
                                } else {
                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 26, -57; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_basesideleft.png", 26, -57; }

                                    IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 28, -55; }
                                    else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 28, -55; }

                                    DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 31, -73, 2;
                                }
                            }
                        } else {
                            InInventory PowerSpeed && PowerInvulnerable
                            {
                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 70, -57; }

                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 72, -55; }

                                DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 75, -73, 2;
                            } else InInventory PowerSpeed || PowerInvulnerable {
                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 48, -57; }

                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 50, -55; }

                                DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 53, -73, 2;
                            } else {
                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_base.png", 26, -57; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_basesideleft.png", 26, -57; }

                                IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 28, -55; }
                                else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/timers/goodolhud_timer_fire.png", 28, -55; }

                                DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Fire, PowerupTime ArtiTorch, DrawShadow, Alignment(Center), 31, -73, 2;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Top right.
    IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal { DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Untranslated, Time, -70, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right); }

    GameMode SinglePlayer, Cooperative
    {
        IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal
        {
            IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
            {
                DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, "$GOODOLHUD_MONSTERS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, Kills, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, Monsters, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
            } else {
                DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, "$GOODOLHUD_MONSTERS", -102, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, Kills, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 0, 2;
                DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Brick, Monsters, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 0, 2;
            }
        }

        IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal
        {
            IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal
            {
                IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SECRETS", -102, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, Secrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 32, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, TotalSecrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 32, 2;
                } else {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SECRETS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, Secrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, TotalSecrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
                }
            } else {
                IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SECRETS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, Secrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, TotalSecrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
                } else {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SECRETS", -102, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, Secrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 0, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Yellow, TotalSecrets, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 0, 2;
                }
            }
        }

        IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal
        {
            IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal
            {
                IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal
                {
                    IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                    {
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 48, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 48, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 48, 2;
                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 48, 2;
                    } else {
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 32, 2;
                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 32, 2;
                    }
                } else {
                    IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                    {
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 32, 2;
                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 32, 2;
                    } else {
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                        DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                        DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
                    }
                }
            } else IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal {
                IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 32, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 32, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 32, 2;
                } else {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
                }
            } else {
                IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
                {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 16, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 16, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 16, 2;
                } else {
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_ITEMS", -102, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
                    DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, "$GOODOLHUD_SEPARATOR", -46, 0, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);

                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, Items, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right), -54, 0, 2;
                    DrawNumber 5, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", LightBlue, TotalItems, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), -46, 0, 2;
                }
            }
        }

        IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal
        {
            IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal
            {
                IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal
                {
                    IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 68; }
                    else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 52; }
                }
                else IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 52; }
                else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
            } else IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal {
                IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 52; }
                else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
            }
            else IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
            else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 20; }
        } else {
            IfCVarInt goh_showmonstercounter, 1, equal
            {
                IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal
                {
                    IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 52; }
                    else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
                }
                else IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
                else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 20; }
            } else IfCVarInt goh_showsecretcounter, 1, equal {
                IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 36; }
                else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 20; }
            }
            else IfCVarInt goh_showitemcounter, 1, equal { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 20; }
            else { DrawKeyBar 100, Vertical, Auto, -26, 4; }
        }
    }

    GameMode Deathmatch, TeamGame
    {
        IfCVarInt goh_showtimer, 1, equal { DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Untranslated, Frags, DrawShadow, -6, 16, 2; }
        else { DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Untranslated, Frags, DrawShadow, -6, 0, 2; }
    }

    // Top center.
    IfCVarInt goh_showairtimer, 1, equal
    {
        IfWaterLevel 3
        {
            IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme0/bars/goodolhud_bar_base.png", -73 + Center, 60; }
            else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawImage "graphics/hud/theme1/bars/goodolhud_bar_base.png", -73 + Center, 60; }

            IfCVarInt not goh_theme, 1 { DrawBar "graphics/hud/theme0/bars/goodolhud_bar_blue.png", "graphics/hud/theme0/bars/goodolhud_bar_blank.png", AirTime, Horizontal, -72 + Center, 61; }
            else IfCVarInt goh_theme, 1 { DrawBar "graphics/hud/theme1/bars/goodolhud_bar_blue.png", "graphics/hud/theme1/bars/goodolhud_bar_blank.png", AirTime, Horizontal, -72 + Center, 61; }

            DrawString "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Blue, "$GOODOLHUD_OXYGEN", -79 + Center, 63, 2, DrawShadow, Alignment(Right);
            DrawNumber 4, "fonts/goodolhud_font.bmf", Blue, AirTime, DrawShadow, Alignment(Left), 82 + Center, 63, 2;
        }
    }

    else { DrawInventoryBar Hexen, 7, INDEXFONT, 50, 170, 76, 192, White; }
